    <script>
			window.applyWorkingExceptions = function() {
		// console.log('applying working exception....');
		var _working_exceptions = $('#calendar').data('working_exceptions');
		var events_to_hide = [];
		_working_exceptions.forEach(function(working_exception) {
			// console.log(working_exception);
			if (calendar !== undefined) {
				//find events that need to be hidden due to working exceptions
				(calendar.getEvents()).forEach(function(event) {
					if ( (moment(event.start).format('YYYY-MM-DD HH:mm:ss') >= moment(working_exception.valid_since).format('YYYY-MM-DD HH:mm:ss')) && ((moment(event.end).format('YYYY-MM-DD HH:mm:ss') <= moment(working_exception.valid_to).format('YYYY-MM-DD HH:mm:ss'))) ) {
						if (event.rendering != 'background'){
							console.log(event);
							events_to_hide.push(event);
						}
					}
					//console.log('event starts:...' + event.start + ' / ends: ...' + event.end);
				});
			}
			
			
			
			
			//hide events from exceptions
			switch(true) {
				case ($('.fc-dayGridMonth-view').length == 1):  //month
					events_to_hide.forEach(function(event){
						const event_start = moment(event.start).day();
						var event_date = moment(event.start).format('YYYY-MM-DD');
						var fc_day_top = $('.fc-day-top[data-date='+event_date+']');
						var fc_week = $(fc_day_top).closest('.fc-row.fc-week');
						var fc_content_skeleton_tr = $(fc_week).find('.fc-content-skeleton table tbody tr');
						fc_content_skeleton_tr.each(function (index){
							var tds = $(this).find('td.fc-event-container');
							$(tds[event_start-1]).find('.fc-event').addClass('hidden');
							var more = $(this).find('td.fc-more-cell');
							$(more[event_start-1]).find('.fc-more').addClass('hidden');
						})
					})
					break;


				case ($('.fc-timeGridWeekDay-view').length == 1):  //week
					//estimate days with hidden events
					var days_to_hide = [];
					events_to_hide.forEach(function (event) {
						//console.log(event);
						const event_start = moment(event.start); 
						if (days_to_hide.indexOf(event_start.day())==-1)
							days_to_hide.push(event_start.day());
					});
					//console.log(days_to_hide);		
					
					days_to_hide.forEach(function(day) {
						$($('.fc-content-skeleton .fc-content-col')[day-1]).find('.fc-event').addClass('hidden');
					});
					break;
					

				case ($('.fc-timeGridDay-view').length == 1):  //day
					if (moment(calendar.view.currentStart).format('YYYY-MM-DD HH:mm:ss') >= moment(working_exception.valid_since).format('YYYY-MM-DD HH:mm:ss'))
						$('.fc-content-skeleton .fc-event').addClass('hidden');
					break;
				
				
				case ($('.fc-listDay-view').length == 1):
					if (moment(calendar.view.currentStart).format('YYYY-MM-DD HH:mm:ss') >= moment(working_exception.valid_since).format('YYYY-MM-DD HH:mm:ss'))
						$('.fc-list-table  .fc-list-item').addClass('hidden');
					break;
			}
		})
	}


	window.applyWorkingExceptionsBlocks = function() {
		console.log('applying working exception BLOCKS....');
		var _working_exceptions = $('#calendar').data('working_exceptions');
		var events_to_hide = [];
		_working_exceptions.forEach(function(working_exception) {
			//console.log(working_exception);
			
			event = {
				title: working_exception.comments,
				description: working_exception.comments,
				start: working_exception.valid_since,
				end: working_exception.valid_to,
				allDay: false,
				rendering: 'background',
				resourceId: 'blocked',
				extendedProps:{
					description: working_exception.comments,
					course_name: working_exception.comments,
					professor: '',
				}
			};
			window.calendar.addEvent(event);
			applyWorkingExceptions();
		});
	}
	
	
	window.relistEventsLegents = function () {
		
		if ($('.fc-timeGridDay-view').length != 1) return;
		
		
		console.log('getting legends');
		var events_to_show = [];
	
		if (calendar !== undefined) {
			//var currentDate = calendar('getDate');
			var currentDate = moment(calendar.getDate()).format('YYYY-MM-DD');
			var lengend_time_window_since = currentDate + " " + "";
			var lengend_time_window_valid_to = currentDate + " " + "";
			
			//find events that need to be shown to legend website part
			(calendar.getEvents()).forEach(function(event) {
				if ( ( (moment(event.start).format('YYYY-MM-DD HH:mm:ss') >= moment(lengend_time_window_since).format('YYYY-MM-DD HH:mm:ss')) && ((moment(event.end).format('YYYY-MM-DD HH:mm:ss') <= moment(lengend_time_window_valid_to).format('YYYY-MM-DD HH:mm:ss'))) ) || 
				( (moment(event.start).format('YYYY-MM-DD HH:mm:ss') >= moment(lengend_time_window_since).format('YYYY-MM-DD HH:mm:ss')) && ((moment(event.start).format('YYYY-MM-DD HH:mm:ss') <= moment(lengend_time_window_valid_to).format('YYYY-MM-DD HH:mm:ss'))) ) ||
				( (moment(event.end).format('YYYY-MM-DD HH:mm:ss') >= moment(lengend_time_window_since).format('YYYY-MM-DD HH:mm:ss')) && ((moment(event.end).format('YYYY-MM-DD HH:mm:ss') <= moment(lengend_time_window_valid_to).format('YYYY-MM-DD HH:mm:ss'))) )
				) {
					if (event.rendering != 'background'){
						events_to_show.push(event);
					}
				}
				
			});
			$('#calendar_legends').html("");
			if (events_to_show.length > 0) {
				//$('.fc-time-grid .fc-slats td').css('height', '84px');
				var currentDay = moment(calendar.getDate()).format('dddd, LL');
				var table_header = "<table id='calendar_legends_table'><tr class='header'><th>" + currentDay + "</th></tr></table>";
				$('#calendar_legends').append(table_header);
				events_to_show.forEach(function(event) {
					let _event_course_name_pieces = event.extendedProps.course_name.split(' - ');
					if (_event_course_name_pieces[1] !== undefined)
						var _event_course_name = _event_course_name_pieces[1];
					else
						var _event_course_name = "";

					for (var i_piece=2; i_piece<=_event_course_name_pieces.length-1; i_piece++) {
						_event_course_name += " - " + _event_course_name_pieces[i_piece];
					};

					var str_legend_event = "<tr class='course' style='background-color: " + event.backgroundColor + "; color:" + event.textColor + "'><td>" + moment(event.start).format('HH:mm') + " - " + moment(event.end).format('HH:mm')  +" &nbsp;&nbsp; " + _event_course_name + " <span class='fa fa-map-marker-alt' style='margin-left: 10px;'></span> "  + event.extendedProps.area_name + "</td></tr>";
					//var str_legend_event = "<tr class='course'><td><span>" + moment(event.start).format('HH:mm') + " - " + moment(event.end).format('HH:mm') +  "<span class='legend_color_mark' style='background-color: " + event.backgroundColor + "'></span></span><span>" + event.extendedProps.area_name + " - " + event.extendedProps.course_name + "</span></td></tr>";
					$('#calendar_legends_table').append(str_legend_event);
				});


				//var event_width = parseFloat($($('.fc-event')[1]).css('left'));
				var next_x_pos = 0;
				var next_y_pos = 0;
				var i_event = 1;
				var multiplier = 3;
				//console.log(event_width);
				//console.log($($('.fc-event')[0]));


			}
		}
	}

				eventRender: function (i) {
					//console.log(i.event);
					let professor = i.event.professor || i.event.extendedProps.professor || '';
					let description = i.event.description || i.event.extendedProps.description || '';
					let _start = i.event.start;
					let _end = i.event.end;
					//console.log(moment(_end).diff(moment(_start)));
					if (moment(_start).format('ss')==1) {
						//console.log('sunstract 1 sec');
						var time = moment.duration("00:00:01");
						_start = moment(_start).subtract(time);
					}
					let duration = moment.utc( moment(_end).diff(moment(_start))).format('H:mm');

						<div>
							<label></label>
							${moment(_start).format('HH:mm')} - ${moment(_end).format('HH:mm')} (${duration})
						</div>`;
						if ((i.event.extendedProps.area_name !="") && (typeof(i.event.extendedProps.area_name) !="undefined")){
							content += `<div>
								<label>Αίθουσα: </label>
								${i.event.extendedProps.area_name}
							</div>`;
						}
						content +=`<div>`;
						if ((i.event.extendedProps.professor !="") && (typeof(i.event.extendedProps.professor) !="undefined")){
						content += `<div>
							<label>Διδάσκων: </label>
							${i.event.extendedProps.professor}
						</div>`;
						}
						if ((i.event.extendedProps.comments !="") && (typeof(i.event.extendedProps.comments) !="undefined")){
						content += `<div>
							<label></label>
							${i.event.extendedProps.comments}
						</div>`;
						}	
						content += `</div>`;
					
                    var tooltip = new Tooltip(i.el, {
                        html: true,
                        title: content,
                        placement: 'top',
                        trigger: 'hover',
                        container: 'body'
                    });
                },

<script>
// Used to toggle the menu on smaller screens when clicking on the menu button
function openNav() {
  var x = document.getElementById("navDemo");
  if (x.className.indexOf("w3-show") == -1) {
    x.className += " w3-show";
  } else { 
    x.className = x.className.replace(" w3-show", "");
  }
}
</script><script>
	$(document).ready(function() {
		var $eventSelect = $("#mydragable_courses_new");
		$eventSelect.select2({
			createTag: function (params) {
				// Return null to disable tag creation
				return null;
			},
			
			templateSelection: function (data, container) {
				//hide all elements
				for (i=0; i<$('#mydragable_courses_new').find(':not(:selected)').length; i++) {
					var _event = $('#mydragable_courses_new').find(':not(:selected)')[i].value;
					$('.' + _event).addClass('hidden');
				}
				$('.fc-event').addClass('hidden');
				for (i=0; i<$('#mydragable_courses_new').find(':selected').length; i++) {
					var _event = $('#mydragable_courses_new').find(':selected')[i].value;
					$('.' + _event).removeClass('hidden');
					$(container).css("background-color", $('#mydragable_courses_new').find(':selected')[i].style.backgroundColor);
					$(container).css("color", $('#mydragable_courses_new').find(':selected')[i].style.color);					
				}
				return data.text;
			}
		});
		
			
		$eventSelect.on('select2:unselecting', function (e) {
			if ($('#mydragable_courses_new').find(':selected').length==1) {
				for (i=0; i<$('#mydragable_courses_new').find(':selected').length; i++) {
					var _event = $('#mydragable_courses_new').find(':selected')[i].value;
					$('.' + _event).addClass('hidden');
				}
			}
		});
	});
</script>
